You're viewing program information for local students.

Not a local student?

RMIT considers you a local student if you are:

  • a citizen or permanent resident of Australia, or
  • a New Zealand citizen, or
  • a Temporary Protection visa (TPV) holder.

If you are unsure or hold a different visa type, please contact Info Corner for more information.

You’re viewing program information for international students.

Not an international student?

RMIT considers you an international student if you are:

  • intending to study on a student visa, or
  • not a citizen or permanent resident of Australia, or
  • not a New Zealand citizen, or
  • not a Temporary Protection visa (TPV) holder.

If you are unsure or hold a different visa type, please contact Info Corner for more information.

Create a personalised brochure

Foundation Studies has been designed to provide international students with an academic entry pathway to first year undergraduate study or its equivalent.

Foundation Studies is developed and accredited by RMIT University and delivered by RMIT University staff at our campus in the heart of Melbourne city.

Foundation Studies students are students of RMIT University from day one of their program, enjoying full membership of a vibrant student community in one of the world’s most liveable cities.

Expand all sections

Duration

52 weeks over 3 teaching periods.

35 weeks over 2 teaching periods.

Duration

Choose to study the Standard program (three trimesters) or Accelerated program (two trimesters)

Standard - 52 weeks over 3 teaching periods.

Accelerated - 35 weeks over 2 teaching periods.

Multiple campuses

Learning and teaching

RMIT offers a variety of learning and teaching approaches including lectures, seminars, studios, workshops, presentations, group discussions and syndicate work. These are primarily in English.

You will have access to the Learning Hub and other online and digital resources through the myRMIT student portal.

Ongoing assessment throughout the semester includes examinations, essays, reports, oral classes, presentations, group projects, research projects, laboratory projects and practical assignments.

Industry connections

The RMIT Foundation Studies Program meets Australia’s National Standards for Foundation Programs. That means it is nationally recognized as a program that equips international students with the skills and capabilities to seek entry into higher education programs in Australia. The program meets the requirements for Foundation Programs that have been registered on CRICOS for delivery in Australia to overseas students providing an academic preparation for seeking entry to first year undergraduate study or its equivalent.



Career outlook

Professional recognition and accreditation

International opportunities

RMIT graduates can earn internationally recognised qualifications at our campuses in Melbourne and Vietnam and through programs delivered at other locations around the world. Our worldwide industry connections stretch across more than 150 educational partners and world-class research institutes. Importantly we also offer financial support, scholarships and grants to support you in your overseas study and travel adventures.

Key people

Contact

Foundation Studies is available to international students only.

Program and course information

  • For current students

Program structure

Local students International students Change

You can choose from the following: 

  • Art, Design and Architecture stream
  • Business stream
  • Science, Engineering and Health stream
  • General program

All Foundation Studies students complete the same four core courses designed to build the language and academic skills you will need for further study.

Discipline stream students complete selected courses which are tailored to prepare you for further study in the field of your choice.  If you have not decided on your future field of study or are looking for a wider course options the General program will be the destination for you.

All Foundation Studies students can choose electives from over 30 courses in multiple fields of study.  Find out more about Foundation Studies electives by visiting the Elective Bank.

Study at your own pace, either Standard (52 weeks over three trimesters) or Accelerated (35 weeks over two trimesters) for any stream or program.

You can start when you're ready with two intakes to choose from. Semesters commence in February and June each year.

 

See the table below for program and stream plans.

Find out more about Foundation Studies.

How to apply

Local students International students Change

Intakes

Applications close date

Intakes

July 2016, February 2017, July 2017, February 2018, July 2018

Applications close date

Steps to apply

Foundation Studies is available to international students only.



Steps to apply

1. Check program entry requirements and confirm you're eligible.

2. Ensure you have your supporting documents ready - this includes certified copies of all academic transcripts.

3. You can either submit your application using iApply online or use a registered RMIT representative in your country.

There are no application deadlines for international students; however, we encourage you to apply early as acceptance into programs is subject to the availability of places. An application fee may apply.

Learn more about the International application process.

February 2017, June 2017

February 2016, June 2016, February 2017, June 2017

February 2016, June 2016, February 2017, June 2017

FS016SEH - Foundation Studies Science, Engineering and Health Stream (Standard)
February 2016, June 2016, February 2017, June 2017

FS016SEHA - Foundation Studies Science, Engineering and Health Stream (Accelerated)
February 2016, June 2016, February 2017, June 2017

Entry requirements

Local students International students Change

Standard program

You must have successfully completed an Australian Year 11, or equivalent with a D average or better.

For information on international qualifications and corresponding entry requirements that are equivalent to an Australian Year 11, see the Entry requirements by country web page.

Accelerated program

You must have successfully completed an Australian Year 11, or equivalent with a C average or better.

For information on international qualifications and corresponding entry requirements that are equivalent to an Australian Year 11, see the Entry requirements by country web page.

Standard program

You must have successfully completed an Australian Year 11, or equivalent with a D average or better.

For information on international qualifications and corresponding entry requirements that are equivalent to an Australian Year 11, see the Entry requirements by country web page.

Accelerated program

You must have successfully completed an Australian Year 11, or equivalent with a C average or better.

For information on international qualifications and corresponding entry requirements that are equivalent to an Australian Year 11, see the Entry requirements by country web page.

Prerequisites

Prerequisites

Selection tasks

Selection tasks

English language requirements

Standard program

To study this program you will need to complete one of the following English proficiency tests:

  • IELTS (Academic): minimum overall band of 5.5 (with no individual band below 5.0)
  • TOEFL (Paper Based Test): minimum score of 530 (TWE 3.5)
  • TOEFL (Internet Based Test - IBT): minimum overall score of 71 (with minimum of 17 in all sections)
  • Pearson Test of English (Academic) (PTE (A)): minimum score of 42 (with no communication band less than 36)
  • Cambridge English: Advanced (CAE): minimum of 162 with no less than 154 in any component.

For detailed information on English language requirements and other proficiency tests recognised by RMIT, visit English language requirements and equivalency information.

Don't meet the English language test scores? Complete an Upper Intermediate Certificate at RMIT English Worldwide.

Accelerated program

To study this program you will need to complete one of the following English proficiency tests:

  • IELTS (Academic): minimum overall band of 5.5 (with no individual band below 5.5)
  • TOEFL (Paper Based Test): minimum score of 535 (TWE 4.0)
  • TOEFL (Internet Based Test - IBT): minimum overall score of 75 (with minimum of 18 in all sections)
  • Pearson Test of English (Academic) (PTE (A)): minimum score of 46 (with no communication band less than 40)
  • Cambridge English: Advanced (CAE): minimum of 162 with no less than 162 in any component.

For detailed information on English language requirements and other proficiency tests recognised by RMIT, visit English language requirements and equivalency information.

Don't meet the English language test scores? Complete an Upper Intermediate Certificate (with no skills below D) at RMIT English Worldwide.

Fees

Local students International students Change

Foundation Studies is available to international students only.



The total indicative tuition fee for 2016 commencement is AU$21,750.

View tuition fees for future years.

Additional expenses

Additional expenses

Other costs
In addition to tuition fees you also need to pay for:

  • Student services and amenities fee (SSAF) in each calendar year.
  • Overseas Student Health Cover (OSHC) - Student visa holders must have cover for the total duration of their visa.
  • Some programs incur additional expenses.

You also need to account for your living expenses. Estimate the cost of living in Melbourne.

Important fee information
Find out more details about how fees are calculated and the expected annual increase.

Scholarships

Local students International students Change

Each year, scholarships are awarded to new Foundation Studies students on the basis of academic merit and personal achievement. Scholarships are open to students from all
countries.

To be eligible you must:

  • be an international student
  • be studying Foundation Studies at RMIT
  • display high standards of academic merit and personal achievement.
  • willing to be involved in RMIT activities beyond your academic program

Read more on Foundation Studies Scholarships

Pathways

Local students International students Change

 



RMIT's Foundation Studies program is specifically designed to provide you with a pathway into a range of RMIT vocational education and undergraduate programs.

It is important that you enrol in the correct Foundation Studies courses to allow you to progress to your preferred vocational education or undergraduate program. Your Program Advisor will be able to advise you on the courses you should enrol in and any specific entry requirements the programs may have (e.g. minimum GPA, pre-requisite courses, folio etc.)

For a full list of programs please see the Guaranteed pathway requirements.
